GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A*exp(-c3*_s*t) + c4*_z*A**c5/(c6*A**c7 + c8)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function of two variables \(t,A\):
\[
F(t,A)= -0.2092477763\,A^2\;+\;\frac{0.2152861754\,A^2}{0.9716398998\,A^4+1}\;-\;0.2092477763\,A\,e^{-0.06535116587\,t}.
\]
Key structural facts:
- It has **exactly one \(t\)-dependent term**, and it is **linear in \(A\)** times a **pure exponential in \(t\)** with **negative rate**: \(-k\,A\,e^{-\lambda t}\).
- The remaining \(A\)-only part is \(-kA^2 + \dfrac{k' A^2}{1+\alpha A^4}\), i.e. a rational function in \(A\) with denominator \(1+\alpha A^4\).
- No \(\sin\), \(\log\), \(\max\), \(\mathrm{Abs}\), etc.

Below, for each candidate, check whether its available building blocks can be parameter-set to reproduce (i) the \(A e^{-\lambda t}\) term and (ii) the specific rational \(A^2/(1+\alpha A^4)\) term, **without introducing extra nonzero terms**.

---

### 1. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2\sin(\cdot)+c5 + c6 e^{c7 t}\sin(\cdot)\)
Can set all sine terms to 0 (e.g., \(c2=0,c6=0\)) and constant \(c5=0\), leaving \(A^2c0+Ac1\). But GT needs a rational \(A^2/(1+\alpha A^4)\) and a \(t\)-dependent \(A e^{-\lambda t}\). Not possible. **No match**.

### 2. Adds \(c5 e^{c6 t}\) and a saturating \(\frac{\max(0,A)^{c8}}{c9+\max(0,A)^{c8}}\)
The saturating term cannot equal \(\frac{A^2}{1+\alpha A^4}\) for all real \(A\) (also uses \(\max(0,A)\), causing piecewise behavior; GT is analytic in \(A\)). Also \(t\)-dependence is only \(c5 e^{c6 t}\) (not multiplied by \(A\)). **No match**.

### 3. Has \(A^{c2}c3 e^{c4 t}\) and a \(\log(\cdot)\)
Could try \(A^{c2}e^{c4 t}\) to mimic \(A e^{-\lambda t}\) by setting \(c2=1,c4=-\lambda\). But then still lacks the rational \(A^2/(1+\alpha A^4)\); log term must be zeroed (\(c6=0\)), leaving only polynomial + \(A e^{-\lambda t}\). Missing rational term. **No match**.

### 4. Contains \(A c0/(A+c1)\), \(A c2\), \(e^{A c4}\), and log-of-exp-of-exp
No way to produce \(\frac{A^2}{1+\alpha A^4}\) exactly; also \(t\) does not appear in the needed way. **No match**.

### 5. Has \(A^2c0+Ac1+c2\) plus saturating Max term plus \(\log(\exp(A\cdot + t\cdot)+1)\)
GT has no \(\log\) and no \(\max\). Zeroing log (\(c6=0\)) still leaves saturating Max term which cannot equal \(A^2/(1+\alpha A^4)\) globally and is piecewise. Also no \(A e^{-\lambda t}\) term. **No match**.

No \(A e^{-\lambda t}\) (the exponential term is not multiplied by \(A\) unless via other factors, which are absent). Also no correct rational term. **No match**.
